Sheila Gandhi was born into a family that valued education above all else when she grew up with her parents’ emphasis being placed upon learning from books rather than television or other media sources which were not widely available back then.. Her love affair began early enough too since age six where Sheila would read over half-a-dozen novels every week! With such dedication growing stronger each day more stories unfolded within these pages until they became part-time jobs after college graduation due largely because there weren’t many job openings left so now work freelance writing full time while still pursuing new projects across genres including fiction short story collection called ‘The Artisan's Journey’. This book showcases how life experiences shape us through trials like hers during times filled w ith uncertainty yet ultimately lead towards personal growth despite setbacks along way. It also touches topics relevant today, offering fresh perspectives gained via travel around world exploring diverse cultures before settling down permanently somewhere between Mumbai Andhra Pradesh! As someone said "A good writer should be able write anything" but what about those moments you wish could've written something better? Here lies another aspect explored deeply throughout 'Artisans'.  <b><u>Lokapriya Sankulam - Buddha Statue </U>, Budharath Road, Mahadevapura Village<br></b>&nbsp;
Mahabodhi Temple is one of the most sacred Buddhist sites on earth and it's also known as Lokpriyaa Shankula or Lopai Sri Maha Bodha Giri / Buddhasaradhara Shanti Stupa. It was built by Indian Government to commemorate India’s contribution towards World Peace which has been recognized at national level for its efforts toward peace through art therapy since year 2007.
It located near Bangalore International Airport with easy access from major cities like Hyderabad, Mumbai, Delhi etc.
This statue stands over 80 feet tall that can be seen clearly during day time but when night falls due to LED lightings around this area you will feel mesmerized watching these beautiful statues under starry sky.
